\section*{Joltage machines â€” ILP/CP-SAT model + solutions}
% Machine 1
\subsection*{Machine 1}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[#.......#]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{8,27,38,16,29,6,33,24,29\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{2,4\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{1,2,6,8\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{2,5,6,7\}$
\item $x_{3}$ affects $\{0,1,2,4,6,7,8\}$
\item $x_{4}$ affects $\{3,8\}$
\item $x_{5}$ affects $\{0,3,4,5,6,8\}$
\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{1,2,4,6,7\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{6} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,8 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{3} + x_{5} &= 8 \\
x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{6} &= 27 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{6} &= 38 \\
x_{4} + x_{5} &= 16 \\
x_{0} + x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 29 \\
x_{2} + x_{5} &= 6 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 33 \\
x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{6} &= 24 \\
x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} &= 29 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} &= 7 \\
x_{1} &= 7 \\
x_{2} &= 4 \\
x_{3} &= 6 \\
x_{4} &= 14 \\
x_{5} &= 2 \\
x_{6} &= 14 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 54\\

% Machine 2
\subsection*{Machine 2}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[###.]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{27,12,27,21\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{0,1,2\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{0,2,3\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{1,3\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{2} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,3 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} + x_{1} &= 27 \\
x_{0} + x_{2} &= 12 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} &= 27 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} &= 21 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} &= 9 \\
x_{1} &= 18 \\
x_{2} &= 3 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 30\\

% Machine 3
\subsection*{Machine 3}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[.#.#]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{159,164,159,5\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{1,3\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{0,1,2\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{1} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,3 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{1} &= 159 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} &= 164 \\
x_{1} &= 159 \\
x_{0} &= 5 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} &= 5 \\
x_{1} &= 159 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 164\\

% Machine 4
\subsection*{Machine 4}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[.###.##]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{174,170,59,170,162,170,26\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{1,2\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,5\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{2,3,5\}$
\item $x_{3}$ affects $\{2,4,6\}$
\item $x_{4}$ affects $\{0,2,6\}$
\item $x_{5}$ affects $\{0,1,3,4,5\}$
\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,4,5\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{6} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,6 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{1} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 174 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 170 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{6} &= 59 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 170 \\
x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 162 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 170 \\
x_{3} + x_{4} &= 26 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{1} &= 30 \\
x_{3} &= 22 \\
x_{4} &= 4 \\
x_{5} &= 137 \\
x_{6} &= 3 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 196\\

% Machine 5
\subsection*{Machine 5}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[...##..##.]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{37,46,35,37,24,37,19,16,9,35\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{0,1,2,4,6,9\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,4,5,6,9\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{0,1,2,5,9\}$
\item $x_{3}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,7\}$
\item $x_{4}$ affects $\{0,1,3,6,8\}$
\item $x_{5}$ affects $\{3,5\}$
\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{1,3,4,5,6,9\}$
\item $x_{7}$ affects $\{1,3,4,5,7,8,9\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{7} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,9 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} &= 37 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 46 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} &= 35 \\
x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 37 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 24 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{5} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 37 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{4} + x_{6} &= 19 \\
x_{3} + x_{7} &= 16 \\
x_{4} + x_{7} &= 9 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 35 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{1} &= 15 \\
x_{2} &= 11 \\
x_{3} &= 9 \\
x_{4} &= 2 \\
x_{5} &= 2 \\
x_{6} &= 2 \\
x_{7} &= 7 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 48\\

% Machine 6
\subsection*{Machine 6}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[#...#.####]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{58,53,44,44,10,63,26,32,38,44\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{1,3,4,6,8\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{0,1,4,5,6,9\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{1,5,6\}$
\item $x_{3}$ affects $\{3,4,5,8\}$
\item $x_{4}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,5,6,8,9\}$
\item $x_{5}$ affects $\{0,2,3,9\}$
\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,5,7,9\}$
\item $x_{7}$ affects $\{0,2,4,5,7,8,9\}$
\item $x_{8}$ affects $\{0,1,5,7,8\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{8} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,9 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{1} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} + x_{7} + x_{8} &= 58 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{4} + x_{6} + x_{8} &= 53 \\
x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 44 \\
x_{0} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 44 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{7} &= 10 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{6} + x_{7} + x_{8} &= 63 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{4} &= 26 \\
x_{6} + x_{7} + x_{8} &= 32 \\
x_{0} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{7} + x_{8} &= 38 \\
x_{1} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 44 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{2} &= 12 \\
x_{3} &= 5 \\
x_{4} &= 14 \\
x_{5} &= 12 \\
x_{6} &= 13 \\
x_{7} &= 5 \\
x_{8} &= 14 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 75\\

% Machine 7
\subsection*{Machine 7}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[.....##..#]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{33,42,33,14,58,14,26,32,46,28\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{0,1,3,4,6,7,8,9\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{1,4,5,6,8,9\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{0,3,9\}$
\item $x_{3}$ affects $\{0,1,4,7,8,9\}$
\item $x_{4}$ affects $\{2,4,7\}$
\item $x_{5}$ affects $\{1,8\}$
\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{0,2,3,7,8,9\}$
\item $x_{7}$ affects $\{0,4,5,6,7,8,9\}$
\item $x_{8}$ affects $\{0,1,2,4,8\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{8} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,9 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{6} + x_{7} + x_{8} &= 33 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{8} &= 42 \\
x_{4} + x_{6} + x_{8} &= 33 \\
x_{0} + x_{2} + x_{6} &= 14 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{7} + x_{8} &= 58 \\
x_{1} + x_{7} &= 14 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{7} &= 26 \\
x_{0} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 32 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{6} + x_{7} + x_{8} &= 46 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 28 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} &= 12 \\
x_{1} &= 11 \\
x_{2} &= 1 \\
x_{4} &= 16 \\
x_{5} &= 3 \\
x_{6} &= 1 \\
x_{7} &= 3 \\
x_{8} &= 16 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 63\\

% Machine 8
\subsection*{Machine 8}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[....#..#.]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{80,77,75,39,56,78,65,47,73\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{0,2,5,8\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{1,3,4,5,6,7,8\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{1,2,3,7\}$
\item $x_{3}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,4,5,6,8\}$
\item $x_{4}$ affects $\{0,1,2,4,6,7\}$
\item $x_{5}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,5,6,7,8\}$
\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{0\}$
\item $x_{7}$ affects $\{0,1,3,5,7,8\}$
\item $x_{8}$ affects $\{0,1,3,4,5,7\}$
\item $x_{9}$ affects $\{0,1,2,4,5,6,8\}$
\item $x_{10}$ affects $\{1,5,6,7,8\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{10} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,8 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} + x_{7} + x_{8} + x_{9} &= 80 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{7} + x_{8} + x_{9} + x_{10} &= 77 \\
x_{0} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{9} &= 75 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{7} + x_{8} &= 39 \\
x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{8} + x_{9} &= 56 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{7} + x_{8} + x_{9} + x_{10} &= 78 \\
x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{9} + x_{10} &= 65 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{7} + x_{8} + x_{10} &= 47 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{7} + x_{9} + x_{10} &= 73 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} &= 16 \\
x_{1} &= 10 \\
x_{2} &= 4 \\
x_{3} &= 3 \\
x_{4} &= 11 \\
x_{5} &= 14 \\
x_{6} &= 1 \\
x_{7} &= 3 \\
x_{8} &= 5 \\
x_{9} &= 27 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 94\\

% Machine 9
\subsection*{Machine 9}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[.#####]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{66,50,21,16,70,64\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{5\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{4,5\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{2,5\}$
\item $x_{3}$ affects $\{0,1,5\}$
\item $x_{4}$ affects $\{0,4\}$
\item $x_{5}$ affects $\{0,1,4,5\}$
\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,4\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{6} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,5 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 66 \\
x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 50 \\
x_{2} + x_{6} &= 21 \\
x_{6} &= 16 \\
x_{1} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 70 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{5} &= 64 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{1} &= 25 \\
x_{2} &= 5 \\
x_{3} &= 21 \\
x_{4} &= 16 \\
x_{5} &= 13 \\
x_{6} &= 16 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 96\\

% Machine 10
\subsection*{Machine 10}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[....####]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{18,43,32,54,60,69,35,15\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{1,4,5\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{1,4\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{2,5\}$
\item $x_{3}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,4,5,6\}$
\item $x_{4}$ affects $\{0,3,4,5,6,7\}$
\item $x_{5}$ affects $\{3,4,5\}$
\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{1,2,3,5,6\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{6} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,7 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{3} + x_{4} &= 18 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{6} &= 43 \\
x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{6} &= 32 \\
x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 54 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} &= 60 \\
x_{0} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 69 \\
x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{6} &= 35 \\
x_{4} &= 15 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} &= 3 \\
x_{1} &= 20 \\
x_{2} &= 12 \\
x_{3} &= 3 \\
x_{4} &= 15 \\
x_{5} &= 19 \\
x_{6} &= 17 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 89\\

% Machine 11
\subsection*{Machine 11}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[.#.#]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{2,194,17,196\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{1,3\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{2\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{0,2,3\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{2} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,3 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{2} &= 2 \\
x_{0} &= 194 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} &= 17 \\
x_{0} + x_{2} &= 196 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} &= 194 \\
x_{1} &= 15 \\
x_{2} &= 2 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 211\\

% Machine 13
\subsection*{Machine 13}
\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[#....#...#]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{77,44,104,72,76,57,91,60,51,44\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{0,1,3,4,6,7,8\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{0,2,3,4,5,6,7\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,4,5,8,9\}$
\item $x_{3}$ affects $\{1,2,3,4,6,7,8,9\}$
\item $x_{4}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,6,7\}$
\item $x_{5}$ affects $\{0,2,5,9\}$
\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{3,7,9\}$
\item $x_{7}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,4,5,8\}$
\item $x_{8}$ affects $\{2\}$
\item $x_{9}$ affects $\{6,8,9\}$
\item $x_{10}$ affects $\{0,2,4,5,6\}$
\item $x_{11}$ affects $\{1,6,8,9\}$
\item $x_{12}$ affects $\{2,3,4,6,7,8,9\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{12} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,9 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{7} + x_{10} &= 77 \\
x_{0} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{7} + x_{11} &= 44 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{7} + x_{8} + x_{10} + x_{12} &= 104 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{6} + x_{7} + x_{12} &= 72 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{7} + x_{10} + x_{12} &= 76 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{5} + x_{7} + x_{10} &= 57 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{9} + x_{10} + x_{11} + x_{12} &= 91 \\

\textbf{Pattern:} \texttt{[#.##.##]}\\
\textbf{Targets:} $\{91,67,38,63,31,58,44\}$\\
\textbf{Buttons:}\\
\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{0,3\}$
\item $x_{1}$ affects $\{1\}$
\item $x_{2}$ affects $\{0,2,4,5\}$
\item $x_{3}$ affects $\{0,1,3,6\}$
\item $x_{4}$ affects $\{0,1,2,3,5\}$
\item $x_{5}$ affects $\{0,1,5,6\}$
\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{0,2,3,4,5\}$
\item $x_{7}$ affects $\{0,3,4,6\}$
\end{itemize}
\[
\begin{aligned}
\min \quad & \sum_{j=0}^{7} x_j \\
\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,6 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 91 \\
x_{1} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} &= 67 \\
x_{2} + x_{4} + x_{6} &= 38 \\
x_{0} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 63 \\
x_{2} + x_{6} + x_{7} &= 31 \\
x_{2} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} &= 58 \\
x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{7} &= 44 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{0} &= 9 \\
x_{1} &= 16 \\
x_{2} &= 8 \\
x_{3} &= 1 \\
x_{4} &= 30 \\
x_{5} &= 20 \\
x_{7} &= 23 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 107\\

\text{s.t.}\quad & \sum_{j \in S_i} x_j = b_i \quad \forall i=0,\dots,9 \\
& x_j \in \mathbb{Z}_{\ge 0}
\end{aligned}
\]
\[
\begin{aligned}
x_{2} + x_{4} + x_{6} + x_{8} &= 31 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{8} + x_{9} &= 37 \\
x_{1} + x_{5} + x_{9} &= 21 \\
x_{0} + x_{2} + x_{4} + x_{9} &= 46 \\
x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{6} + x_{7} + x_{8} + x_{9} &= 69 \\

x_{0} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{6} + x_{7} + x_{9} &= 66 \\
x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{7} + x_{8} + x_{10} &= 44 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{4} + x_{5} + x_{9} + x_{10} &= 58 \\
x_{0} + x_{1} + x_{2} + x_{3} + x_{5} + x_{9} &= 39 \\
\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Solution:} \\
\[
\begin{aligned}

x_{3} &= 10 \\
x_{4} &= 19 \\

\end{aligned}
\]
\textbf{Total presses:} 76\\

\subsection*{Machine 153}

\begin{itemize}
\item $x_{0}$ affects $\{0,2,4,6\}$

\item $x_{6}$ affects $\{0,4,5,6\}$
\item $x_{7}$ affects $\{0,1,2,4,5\}$
\item $x_{8}$ affects $\{1,3,4,5\}$
\end{itemize}

\end{aligned}
